    Hi Bary, 
      
    You’re not alone, these components are tricky to compare so we’re happy to clarify! 
      
    How our proposed solution fits with CloudG and addresses your questions: 
      
    Email Account Administration: We do not provide direct email administration; that remains an IT function for CloudG. However, we do provide alerting and response for events triggered across Azure and their endpoints. 
      
    ITDR & EDR Capabilities: Our solution absolutely covers ITDR. Microsoft provides this natively via Entra ID Protection and Defender for Identity. We will work with Paradigm to ensure these features are enabled and feeding into Azure Sentinel, providing a more unified security posture than a standalone tool like Huntress. 
      
    The Broader MSP Situation: We are designed to be flexible. We can layer our security services on top of CloudG (or any other tier-one MSP). However, if CloudG isn't solving the underlying issues, we have the capability to step in and take on those broader MSP services directly - including managing their Azure and Microsoft 365 environments. 
      
    Let us know if you’d like to jump on a quick call to talk through this. We want to help you be that voice to ensure they get the right solution in place. 
      
    Best, 
    Austin

    Role Designation: We will transition the naming convention from "vCISO" to Security Officer. This aligns with your preference for a clear, simplified appointment that fulfills HIPAA regulatory requirements and streamlines future due diligence. 
      
    Focus Areas: The engagement will focus strictly on the HIPAA Security Rule and bridging the gap between RCS leadership and your third-party IT vendor, Tri-State. 
      
    Strategic ROI: We understand the priority is to maximize ROI by focusing on "material fixes" identified in the pending Security Risk Analysis (SRA). The goal is to ensure a defensible posture for the market without over-engineering solutions that may change post-closing.

[04:33:10 PM CT] [Johnny DM] Johnny (@johnny_forsyth_bot) (edited 04:33 PM)
    Here's what FEED-RULES says about email thread parsing:
    
    **Email Thread Parsing** (applies to Email Feed inputs AND any DM where you forward me an email chain):
    
    1. **Read newest message first** — most recent reply is at the top, that's the new info, start there
    2. **Skip boilerplate** — signatures, legal disclaimers, "Sent from my iPhone", confidentiality notices, auto-generated footers
    3. **Check deal-state before re-analyzing older messages** — read the deal's Communication Log first; anything already logged there is known, don't re-extract or re-summarize it
    4. **Only process what's new** — classification, writes, drafts, and your DM should reflect only genuinely new information, not a re-summary of the entire thread
    
    The core idea: don't re-process what I already know. Hit the newest message, diff it against what's already in the deal-state, and only capture the delta. Why — what's up?

    Hi Bary, 
      
    You’re not alone, these components are tricky to compare so we’re happy to clarify! 
      
    How our proposed solution fits with CloudG and addresses your questions: 
      
    Email Account Administration: We do not provide direct email administration; that remains an IT function for CloudG. However, we do provide alerting and response for events triggered across Azure and their endpoints. 
      
    ITDR & EDR Capabilities: Our solution absolutely covers ITDR. Microsoft provides this natively via Entra ID Protection and Defender for Identity. We will work with Paradigm to ensure these features are enabled and feeding into Azure Sentinel, providing a more unified security posture than a standalone tool like Huntress. 
      
    The Broader MSP Situation: We are designed to be flexible. We can layer our security services on top of CloudG (or any other tier-one MSP). However, if CloudG isn't solving the underlying issues, we have the capability to step in and take on those broader MSP services directly - including managing their Azure and Microsoft 365 environments. 
      
    Let us know if you’d like to jump on a quick call to talk through this. We want to help you be that voice to ensure they get the right solution in place.
